[1mNAME[0m[m
       rm - remove files or directories[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mrm [22m[[4mOPTION[24m]... [[4mFILE[24m]...[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mrm[22m.  [1mrm [22mremoves each spec‐[m
       ified file.  By default, it does not remove directories.[m
[m
       If the [4m-I[24m or [4m--interactive=once[24m option is given, and there are more than[m
       three files or the [4m-r[24m, [4m-R[24m, or [4m--recursive[24m are given, then [1mrm [22mprompts the[m
       user  for whether to proceed with the entire operation.  If the response[m
       is not affirmative, the entire command is aborted.[m
[m
       Otherwise, if a file is unwritable, standard input is  a  terminal,  and[m
       the [4m-f[24m or [4m--force[24m option is not given, or the [4m-i[24m or [4m--interactive=always[0m[m

[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mman [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [[[4msection[24m] [4mpage[24m ...] ...[m
       [1mman -k [22m[[4mapropos[24m [4moptions[24m] [4mregexp[24m ...[m
       [1mman -K [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [[4msection[24m] [4mterm[24m ...[m

       [1mman -l [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [4mfile[24m ...[m
       [1mman -w[22m|[1m-W [22m[[4mman[24m [4moptions[24m] [4mpage[24m ...[m

[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1mman  [22mis  the system's manual pager.  Each [4mpage[24m argument given to [1mman[0m[m
       is normally the name of a program, utility or function.  The  [4mmanual[0m[m
       [4mpage[24m  associated with each of these arguments is then found and dis‐[m
       played.  A [4msection[24m, if provided, will direct [1mman  [22mto  look  only  in[m
